The core principle of FRS 115 is that an entity recognises revenue to depict the transfer'}, {'bbox': '237 749 1497 772', 'page': 67, 'content': 'of promised goods or services to customers in an amount that reflects the consideration to which the entity'}, {'bbox': '237 785 1496 808', 'page': 67, 'content': 'expects to be entitled in exchange for those goods or services.
